    80	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
    81	pub enum DriftAlertCooldownDecision {
    82	    Allowed { suppress_until: DateTime<Utc> },
    83	    Suppressed { suppress_until: DateTime<Utc> },
    84	}
    85	
    86	#[async_trait::async_trait]
    87	pub trait DriftAlertCooldown: Send + Sync {
    88	    async fn check(
    89	        &self,
    90	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
    91	        now: DateTime<Utc>,
    92	    ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error>;
    93	
    94	    async fn record_emitted(
    95	        &self,
    96	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
    97	        emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
    98	        z_score: f32,
    99	    ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error>;
   100	}
   101	
   102	pub struct PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   103	    pool: PgPool,
   104	}
   105	
   106	impl PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   107	    pub fn new(pool: PgPool) -> Self {
   108	        Self { pool }
   109	    }
   110	}
   111	
   112	#[async_trait::async_trait]
   113	impl DriftAlertCooldown for PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore {
   114	    async fn check(
   115	        &self,
   116	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
   117	        now: DateTime<Utc>,
   118	    ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error> {
   119	        let mut tx = self.pool.begin().await.context("begin drift cooldown tx")?;
   120	        sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   121	            .bind(key.tenant_id.to_string())
   122	            .execute(&mut *tx)
   123	            .await
   124	            .context("set RLS tenant_id for prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns")?;
   125	
   126	        let active_until = sqlx::query_scalar::<_, DateTime<Utc>>(
   127	            r#"
   128	            SELECT suppress_until
   129	            FROM prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns
   130	            WHERE tenant_id = $1
   131	              AND model = $2
   132	              AND agent_id = $3
   133	              AND prompt_class = $4
   134	            "#,
   135	        )
   136	        .bind(key.tenant_id)
   137	        .bind(&key.model)
   138	        .bind(&key.agent_id)
   139	        .bind(&key.prompt_class)
   140	        .fetch_optional(&mut *tx)
   141	        .await
   142	        .context("read prediction_drift_alert cooldown")?;
   143	
   144	        let decision = match active_until {
   145	            Some(until) if until > now => DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed {
   146	                suppress_until: until,
   147	            },
   148	            _ => DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed {
   149	                suppress_until: now + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS),
   150	            },
   151	        };
   152	
   153	        tx.commit()
   154	            .await
   155	            .context("commit drift cooldown check tx")?;
   156	        Ok(decision)
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    async fn record_emitted(
   160	        &self,
   161	        key: &DriftAlertKey,
   162	        emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
   163	        z_score: f32,
   164	    ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error> {
   165	        if !z_score.is_finite() {
   166	            anyhow::bail!("non-finite z_score cannot enter drift alert cooldown store");
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        let suppress_until = emitted_at + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   170	        let mut tx = self.pool.begin().await.context("begin drift cooldown tx")?;
   171	        sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   172	            .bind(key.tenant_id.to_string())
   173	            .execute(&mut *tx)
   174	            .await
   175	            .context("set RLS tenant_id for prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns")?;
   176	
   177	        let recorded_until = sqlx::query_scalar::<_, DateTime<Utc>>(
   178	            r#"
   179	            INSERT INTO prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns (
   180	              tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class,
   181	              last_emitted_at, suppress_until, last_z_score, updated_at
   182	            )
   183	            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, clock_timestamp())
   184	            ON CONFLICT (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
   185	              DO UPDATE SET
   186	                last_emitted_at = EXCLUDED.last_emitted_at,
   187	                suppress_until = EXCLUDED.suppress_until,
   188	                last_z_score = EXCLUDED.last_z_score,
   189	                updated_at = clock_timestamp()
   190	            RETURNING suppress_until
   191	            "#,
   192	        )
   193	        .bind(key.tenant_id)
   194	        .bind(&key.model)
   195	        .bind(&key.agent_id)
   196	        .bind(&key.prompt_class)
   197	        .bind(emitted_at)
   198	        .bind(suppress_until)
   199	        .bind(z_score)
   200	        .fetch_one(&mut *tx)
   201	        .await
   202	        .context("record prediction_drift_alert cooldown")?;
   203	
   204	        tx.commit().await.context("commit drift cooldown tx")?;
   205	        Ok(recorded_until)
   206	    }
   207	}
   208	
   209	/// Per spec §7.3 suggested action heuristic.
   210	fn suggest_action(z_score: f32) -> &'static str {
   211	    if z_score > 0.0 {
   212	        "investigate_agent_change"
   213	    } else {
   214	        "review_predictor_baseline"
   215	    }
   216	}
   217	
   218	/// Compute z-score per spec §7.1.
   219	///
   220	/// R2 M2 (Software F5): baseline EXCLUDES the current 7-day window.
   221	/// R1 shape used mean_30d (which includes the last 7d) → baseline was
   222	/// contaminated by the very window we were comparing against, biasing
   223	/// z toward 0. Now we read baseline_mean / baseline_stddev which were
   224	/// computed over [now - 30d, now - 7d] (see aggregation.rs::agg_baseline).
   225	///
   226	/// Returns None when:
   227	///   * 7d window is missing (no current sample to compare)
   228	///   * baseline window is missing (new bucket; first activity in 7d)
   229	///   * baseline_stddev == 0 (all baseline samples identical → undefined ratio)
   230	pub fn compute_z_score(agg: &BucketAggregate) -> Option<f32> {

 succeeded in 0ms:
   640	        // → z = (150 - 100) / 20 = 2.5
   641	        BucketAggregate {
   642	            tenant_id: Uuid::new_v4(),
   643	            model: "gpt-4o".into(),
   644	            agent_id: "agent-a".into(),
   645	            prompt_class: "chat_short".into(),
   646	            mean_7d: Some(150.0),
   647	            stddev_7d: Some(20.0),
   648	            sample_size_7d: Some(200),
   649	            mean_30d: Some(100.0),
   650	            stddev_30d: Some(20.0),
   651	            sample_size_30d: Some(800),
   652	            baseline_mean: Some(100.0),
   653	            baseline_stddev: Some(20.0),
   654	            baseline_sample_size: Some(600),
   655	        }
   656	    }

   663	        assert!((z - 2.5).abs() < 1e-4);

   697	    #[test]
   698	    fn z_score_uses_baseline_excluding_current_window() {
   699	        // R2 M2 regression: mean_30d INCLUDES the current 7d, baseline
   700	        // EXCLUDES it. Verify drift_detector reads from baseline_*
   701	        // (the excluded form), not mean_30d. Construct a case where
   702	        // the two differ + assert the computed z reflects baseline_*.
   703	        let mut agg = fixture_agg();
   704	        agg.mean_30d = Some(140.0); // inclusive mean — close to mean_7d
   705	        agg.stddev_30d = Some(100.0); // inclusive stddev — would damp z
   706	        agg.baseline_mean = Some(100.0); // exclusive baseline
   707	        agg.baseline_stddev = Some(20.0); // exclusive baseline
   708	                                          // z must be (150 - 100) / 20 = 2.5, NOT (150 - 140) / 100 = 0.1.
   709	        let z = compute_z_score(&agg).expect("z");
   710	        assert!((z - 2.5).abs() < 1e-4, "z must use baseline_*, got {z}");
   711	    }

   850	    #[derive(Default)]
   851	    struct MemoryCooldown {
   852	        entries: parking_lot::Mutex<HashMap<DriftAlertKey, DateTime<Utc>>>,
   853	    }
   854	
   855	    #[async_trait::async_trait]
   856	    impl DriftAlertCooldown for MemoryCooldown {
   857	        async fn check(
   858	            &self,
   859	            key: &DriftAlertKey,
   860	            now: DateTime<Utc>,
   861	        ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error> {
   862	            let entries = self.entries.lock();
   863	            if let Some(existing) = entries.get(key) {
   864	                if *existing > now {
   865	                    return Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed {
   866	                        suppress_until: *existing,
   867	                    });
   868	                }
   869	            }
   870	            let suppress_until = now + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   871	            Ok(DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { suppress_until })
   872	        }
   873	
   874	        async fn record_emitted(
   875	            &self,
   876	            key: &DriftAlertKey,
   877	            emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
   878	            _z_score: f32,
   879	        ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error> {
   880	            let suppress_until = emitted_at + ChronoDuration::hours(DRIFT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_HOURS);
   881	            let mut entries = self.entries.lock();
   882	            entries.insert(key.clone(), suppress_until);
   883	            Ok(suppress_until)
   884	        }
   885	    }
   886	
   887	    struct FailingCooldown;
   888	
   889	    #[async_trait::async_trait]
   890	    impl DriftAlertCooldown for FailingCooldown {
   891	        async fn check(
   892	            &self,
   893	            _key: &DriftAlertKey,
   894	            _now: DateTime<Utc>,
   895	        ) -> Result<DriftAlertCooldownDecision, anyhow::Error> {
   896	            Err(anyhow::anyhow!("cooldown store unavailable"))
   897	        }
   898	
   899	        async fn record_emitted(
   900	            &self,
   901	            _key: &DriftAlertKey,
   902	            _emitted_at: DateTime<Utc>,
   903	            _z_score: f32,
   904	        ) -> Result<DateTime<Utc>, anyhow::Error> {
   905	            Err(anyhow::anyhow!("cooldown store unavailable"))
   906	        }
   907	    }
   908	
   909	    #[tokio::test]
   910	    async fn memory_cooldown_suppresses_same_key_until_expiry() {
   911	        let store = MemoryCooldown::default();
   912	        let key = DriftAlertKey::from(&fixture_agg());
   913	        let now = Utc::now();
   914	        let first = store.check(&key, now).await.expect("first");
   915	        assert!(matches!(first, DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }));
   916	        store
   917	            .record_emitted(&key, now, 2.5)
   918	            .await
   919	            .expect("record first");
   920	
   921	        let second = store
   922	            .check(&key, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   923	            .await
   924	            .expect("second");
   925	        assert!(matches!(
   926	            second,
   927	            DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed { .. }

   934	        assert!(matches!(
   935	            after_expiry,
   936	            DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   937	        ));
   938	    }

   969	    fn append_response(status: EventStatus) -> AppendEventsResponse {
   970	        AppendEventsResponse {
   971	            results: vec![EventResult {
   972	                event_id: "evt-1".to_string(),
   973	                status: status as i32,
   974	                ingest_position: None,
   975	                error: Some(ProtoError {
   976	                    code: 0,
   977	                    message: format!("{status:?} for test"),
   978	                    details: Default::default(),
   979	                }),
   980	            }],
   981	        }
   982	    }

  1027	    async fn detect_and_emit_only_fires_on_breach() {
  1028	        use spendguard_signing::DisabledSigner;
  1029	        let sink = RecordingSink {
  1030	            events: parking_lot::Mutex::new(Vec::new()),
  1031	        };
  1032	        let cooldown = MemoryCooldown::default();
  1033	        let signer = DisabledSigner::for_test("test-stats-aggregator".into());
  1034	        let mut breaching = fixture_agg();
  1035	        breaching.mean_7d = Some(200.0); // z = 5.0; far above 2.0
  1036	        let mut normal = fixture_agg();
  1037	        normal.mean_7d = Some(105.0); // z = 0.25; below 2.0
  1038	        let aggregates = vec![breaching, normal];

  1040	            .await
  1041	            .expect("ok");
  1042	        assert_eq!(outcome.emitted, 1, "exactly one breach must fire");
  1043	        assert_eq!(outcome.suppressed, 0);
  1044	        let events = sink.events.lock();
  1045	        assert_eq!(events.len(), 1);
  1046	        assert_eq!(events[0].r#type, PREDICTION_DRIFT_ALERT_EVENT_TYPE);
  1047	    }

     1	-- ============================================================================
     2	-- 0022_prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns.sql — POST_GA_06 drift alert dedup.
     3	--
     4	-- Issues:
     5	--   - #157: 24h cooldown/dedup per (tenant, model, agent_id, prompt_class)
     6	--   - #162: keep non-finite z-scores out of alert state/payloads
     7	--
     8	-- This is mutable derived state owned by stats_aggregator. It gates
     9	-- prediction_drift_alert emission before a new immutable audit event is sent
    10	-- to canonical_ingest, so repeated drift in the same bucket does not spam the
    11	-- audit chain. It deliberately lives beside canonical_events because the
    12	-- stats_aggregator already connects to the canonical DB for aggregation state.
    13	-- ============================================================================
    14	
    15	CREATE TABLE prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns (
    16	    tenant_id       UUID        NOT NULL,
    17	    model           TEXT        NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(model) BETWEEN 1 AND 64),
    18	    agent_id        TEXT        NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(agent_id) BETWEEN 1 AND 128),
    19	    prompt_class    TEXT        NOT NULL CHECK (prompt_class IN (
    20	        'chat_short', 'chat_long', 'code_gen', 'summarization',
    21	        'rag', 'tool_calling', 'vision'
    22	    )),
    23	    last_emitted_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    24	    suppress_until  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    25	    last_z_score    REAL        NOT NULL CHECK (
    26	        last_z_score <> 'NaN'::REAL
    27	        AND last_z_score <> 'Infinity'::REAL
    28	        AND last_z_score <> '-Infinity'::REAL
    29	    ),
    30	    updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT clock_timestamp(),
    31	
    32	    PRIMARY KEY (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class),
    33	    CHECK (suppress_until > last_emitted_at)
    34	);
    35	
    36	CREATE INDEX prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns_suppress_until_idx
    37	    ON prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns (suppress_until);
    38	
    39	ALTER TABLE prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
    40	ALTER TABLE prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
    41	
    42	-- No nil-UUID sentinel: a missing/empty app.current_tenant_id casts to NULL,
    43	-- making the comparison false and the WITH CHECK fail closed.
    44	CREATE POLICY prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns_tenant_isolation
    45	    ON prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns
    46	    FOR ALL
    47	    USING (
    48	        tenant_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_tenant_id', TRUE), '')::uuid
    49	    )
    50	    WITH CHECK (
    51	        tenant_id = NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_tenant_id', TRUE), '')::uuid
    52	    );
    53	
    54	REVOKE SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE ON prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns FROM PUBLIC;
    55	
    56	GRANT SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
    57	    ON prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns
    58	    TO canonical_ingest_application_role;
    59	
    60	GRANT SELECT ON prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns TO canonical_ingest_reader_role;
    61	
    62	COMMENT ON TABLE prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns IS
    63	    'POST_GA_06 mutable dedup state for stats_aggregator prediction_drift_alert CloudEvents. PRIMARY KEY is exactly (tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class); key constraints mirror canonical_events aggregator columns; rows suppress repeat immutable audit alerts for 24h.';
    64	COMMENT ON COLUMN prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns.suppress_until IS
    65	    'Rolling cooldown expiry. stats_aggregator may emit the next alert for the same bucket only when suppress_until <= now().';
    66	COMMENT ON COLUMN prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns.last_z_score IS
    67	    'Finite z-score that triggered the latest emitted alert. CHECK explicitly rejects NaN and +/-Infinity.';
    68

    80	        RAISE EXCEPTION 'prediction_drift_alert_cooldowns_tenant_isolation policy missing';

     1	//! HARDEN_03 / issue #160: real Postgres coverage for the
     2	//! stats_aggregator cycle, cache RLS, and audit-routed drift alert rows.
     3	//!
     4	//! These tests use testcontainers Postgres, apply the canonical_ingest
     5	//! migrations in order, seed canonical_events as the DB owner, then run
     6	//! stats_aggregator queries as a non-superuser member of the canonical
     7	//! application/reader roles. If Docker is unavailable, tests skip with a
     8	//! clear message instead of producing a false negative in local shells.

    35	async fn setup_postgres() -> Option<PgFixture> {
    36	    let container = match Postgres::default().with_tag("16-alpine").start().await {
    37	        Ok(c) => c,
    38	        Err(e) => {
    39	            eprintln!("[stats-aggregator #160] testcontainers Postgres not available: {e}");
    40	            return None;
    41	        }
    42	    };
    43	    let host_port = container
    44	        .get_host_port_ipv4(5432)
    45	        .await
    46	        .expect("postgres host port");
    47	    let owner_url =
    48	        format!("postgres://postgres:postgres@127.0.0.1:{host_port}/postgres?sslmode=disable");
    49	    let app_url =
    50	        format!("postgres://stats_test:stats_test@127.0.0.1:{host_port}/postgres?sslmode=disable");
    51	
    52	    let owner_pool = PgPoolOptions::new()
    53	        .max_connections(5)
    54	        .acquire_timeout(Duration::from_secs(10))
    55	        .connect(&owner_url)
    56	        .await
    57	        .expect("connect owner pool");
    58	
    59	    apply_canonical_migrations(&owner_pool).await;
    60	    create_stats_test_role(&owner_pool).await;
    61	    seed_schema_bundle(&owner_pool).await;
    62	
    63	    let app_pool = PgPoolOptions::new()
    64	        .max_connections(5)
    65	        .acquire_timeout(Duration::from_secs(10))
    66	        .connect(&app_url)
    67	        .await
    68	        .expect("connect app pool");
    69	
    70	    // Keep the container alive for the duration of the test.
    71	    Box::leak(Box::new(container));
    72	
    73	    Some(PgFixture {
    74	        owner_pool,
    75	        app_pool,
    76	    })
    77	}

    79	async fn apply_canonical_migrations(pool: &PgPool) {
    80	    let dir = PathBuf::from(env!("CARGO_MANIFEST_DIR")).join("../canonical_ingest/migrations");
    81	    let mut migrations = fs::read_dir(&dir)
    82	        .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!("read migrations dir {}: {e}", dir.display()))
    83	        .filter_map(|entry| {
    84	            let path = entry.expect("migration entry").path();
    85	            if path.extension().and_then(|s| s.to_str()) == Some("sql") {
    86	                Some(path)
    87	            } else {
    88	                None
    89	            }
    90	        })
    91	        .collect::<Vec<_>>();
    92	    migrations.sort();
    93	
    94	    for path in migrations {
    95	        let sql = fs::read_to_string(&path)
    96	            .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!("read migration {}: {e}", path.display()));
    97	        // sqlx sends a multi-statement migration string as one simple
    98	        // query, which Postgres treats as a single transaction block.
    99	        // Migration 0011 intentionally uses CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY
   100	        // for production online DDL; the test DB is empty and can use a
   101	        // normal CREATE INDEX while preserving the final schema shape.
   102	        let sql = sql.replace("CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY", "CREATE INDEX");
   103	        sqlx::raw_sql(&sql)
   104	            .execute(pool)
   105	            .await
   106	            .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!("apply migration {}: {e}", path.display()));
   107	    }
   108	}

   139	async fn seed_outcome_pair(
   140	    pool: &PgPool,
   141	    tenant_id: Uuid,
   142	    seq: i64,
   143	    age_days: i32,
   144	    actual_output_tokens: i64,
   145	) {

   152	        pool,
   153	        decision_event_id,
   154	        tenant_id,
   155	        Some(decision_id),
   156	        "spendguard.audit.decision",
   157	        age_days,
   158	    )
   159	    .await;
   160	    insert_canonical_event(CanonicalSeed {
   161	        pool,
   162	        event_id: decision_event_id,
   163	        tenant_id,
   164	        decision_id: Some(decision_id),
   165	        run_id: Some(run_id),
   166	        event_type: "spendguard.audit.decision",
   167	        seq: seq * 2,
   168	        age_days,
   169	        actual_input_tokens: None,
   170	        actual_output_tokens: None,
   171	        model: None,
   172	        agent_id: None,
   173	        prompt_class: None,
   174	    })
   175	    .await;
   176	
   177	    insert_global_key(
   178	        pool,
   179	        outcome_event_id,
   180	        tenant_id,
   181	        Some(decision_id),
   182	        "spendguard.audit.outcome",
   183	        age_days,
   184	    )
   185	    .await;
   186	    insert_canonical_event(CanonicalSeed {
   187	        pool,
   188	        event_id: outcome_event_id,
   189	        tenant_id,
   190	        decision_id: Some(decision_id),
   191	        run_id: Some(run_id),
   192	        event_type: "spendguard.audit.outcome",
   193	        seq: seq * 2 + 1,
   194	        age_days,
   195	        actual_input_tokens: Some(42),
   196	        actual_output_tokens: Some(actual_output_tokens),
   197	        model: Some("gpt-4o-mini"),
   198	        agent_id: Some("agent-alpha"),
   199	        prompt_class: Some("chat_short"),
   200	    })
   201	    .await;
   202	}
   203	
   204	async fn seed_sparse_outcome_pair(
   205	    pool: &PgPool,
   206	    tenant_id: Uuid,
   207	    seq: i64,
   208	    age_days: i32,
   209	    actual_output_tokens: i64,
   210	) {
   211	    let decision_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   212	    let run_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   213	    let decision_event_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   214	    let outcome_event_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   215	
   216	    insert_global_key(
   217	        pool,
   218	        decision_event_id,
   219	        tenant_id,
   220	        Some(decision_id),
   221	        "spendguard.audit.decision",
   222	        age_days,
   223	    )
   224	    .await;
   225	    insert_canonical_event(CanonicalSeed {
   226	        pool,
   227	        event_id: decision_event_id,
   228	        tenant_id,
   229	        decision_id: Some(decision_id),
   230	        run_id: Some(run_id),
   231	        event_type: "spendguard.audit.decision",
   232	        seq: seq * 2,
   233	        age_days,
   234	        actual_input_tokens: None,
   235	        actual_output_tokens: None,
   236	        model: Some("gpt-4o-mini"),
   237	        agent_id: Some("agent-alpha"),
   238	        prompt_class: Some("chat_short"),
   239	    })
   240	    .await;
   241	
   242	    insert_global_key(
   243	        pool,
   244	        outcome_event_id,
   245	        tenant_id,
   246	        Some(decision_id),
   247	        "spendguard.audit.outcome",
   248	        age_days,
   249	    )
   250	    .await;
   251	    insert_canonical_event(CanonicalSeed {
   252	        pool,
   253	        event_id: outcome_event_id,
   254	        tenant_id,
   255	        decision_id: Some(decision_id),
   256	        run_id: Some(run_id),
   257	        event_type: "spendguard.audit.outcome",
   258	        seq: seq * 2 + 1,
   259	        age_days,
   260	        actual_input_tokens: Some(42),
   261	        actual_output_tokens: Some(actual_output_tokens),
   262	        model: None,
   263	        agent_id: None,
   264	        prompt_class: None,
   265	    })
   266	    .await;
   267	}
   268	
   269	async fn insert_global_key(
   270	    pool: &PgPool,
   271	    event_id: Uuid,
   272	    tenant_id: Uuid,
   273	    decision_id: Option<Uuid>,
   274	    event_type: &str,
   275	    age_days: i32,
   276	) {
   277	    sqlx::query(
   278	        r#"
   279	        INSERT INTO canonical_events_global_keys (
   280	          event_id, tenant_id, decision_id, event_type, recorded_month, ingest_at
   281	        )
   282	        VALUES (
   283	          $1, $2, $3, $4,
   284	          DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - ($5::INT * interval '1 day'))::DATE,
   285	          now() - ($5::INT * interval '1 day')
   286	        )
   287	        "#,
   288	    )
   289	    .bind(event_id)
   290	    .bind(tenant_id)
   291	    .bind(decision_id)
   292	    .bind(event_type)
   293	    .bind(age_days)
   294	    .execute(pool)
   295	    .await
   296	    .expect("insert canonical_events_global_keys");
   297	}
   298	
   299	struct CanonicalSeed<'a> {
   300	    pool: &'a PgPool,
   301	    event_id: Uuid,
   302	    tenant_id: Uuid,
   303	    decision_id: Option<Uuid>,
   304	    run_id: Option<Uuid>,
   305	    event_type: &'a str,
   306	    seq: i64,
   307	    age_days: i32,
   308	    actual_input_tokens: Option<i64>,
   309	    actual_output_tokens: Option<i64>,
   310	    model: Option<&'a str>,
   311	    agent_id: Option<&'a str>,
   312	    prompt_class: Option<&'a str>,
   313	}
   314	
   315	async fn insert_canonical_event(seed: CanonicalSeed<'_>) {
   316	    sqlx::query(
   317	        r#"
   318	        INSERT INTO canonical_events (
   319	          event_id, tenant_id, decision_id, run_id, event_type, storage_class,
   320	          producer_id, producer_sequence, producer_signature, signing_key_id,
   321	          schema_bundle_id, schema_bundle_hash,
   322	          specversion, source, event_time, datacontenttype, payload_json,
   323	          region_id, ingest_shard_id, ingest_log_offset, ingest_at,
   324	          recorded_month,
   325	          actual_input_tokens, actual_output_tokens,
   326	          model, agent_id, prompt_class, prompt_class_fingerprint, run_id_mirror
   327	        )
   328	        VALUES (
   329	          $1, $2, $3, $4, $5, 'immutable_audit_log',
   330	          'stats-aggregator-test', $6, $7, 'stats-test-key',
   331	          $8, $9,
   332	          '1.0', 'spendguard://stats-aggregator-test',
   333	          now() - ($10::INT * interval '1 day'),
   334	          'application/json', '{}'::jsonb,
   335	          'test-region', 'test-shard', $11,
   336	          now() - ($10::INT * interval '1 day'),
   337	          DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - ($10::INT * interval '1 day'))::DATE,
   338	          $12, $13, $14, $15, $16, $17, $4
   339	        )
   340	        "#,
   341	    )
   342	    .bind(seed.event_id)
   343	    .bind(seed.tenant_id)
   344	    .bind(seed.decision_id)
   345	    .bind(seed.run_id)
   346	    .bind(seed.event_type)
   347	    .bind(seed.seq)
   348	    .bind(vec![0x51_u8, 0x60, 0x61, 0x62])
   349	    .bind(Uuid::parse_str(SCHEMA_BUNDLE_ID).expect("schema bundle uuid"))
   350	    .bind(SCHEMA_BUNDLE_HASH)
   351	    .bind(seed.age_days)
   352	    .bind(seed.seq)
   353	    .bind(seed.actual_input_tokens)
   354	    .bind(seed.actual_output_tokens)
   355	    .bind(seed.model)
   356	    .bind(seed.agent_id)
   357	    .bind(seed.prompt_class)
   358	    .bind(
   359	        seed.prompt_class
   360	            .map(|class| format!("v1:{class}|gpt-4o-mini|1")),
   361	    )
   362	    .execute(seed.pool)
   363	    .await
   364	    .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!("insert canonical_events {}: {e}", seed.event_type));
   365	}
   366	
   367	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   368	async fn cycle_e2e_postgres_populates_output_distribution_cache() {
   369	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   370	        return;
   371	    };
   372	    let tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   373	
   374	    for idx in 0..8 {
   375	        seed_outcome_pair(&fx.owner_pool, tenant_id, idx, 1, 100 + idx).await;
   376	    }
   377	    for idx in 8..16 {
   378	        seed_outcome_pair(&fx.owner_pool, tenant_id, idx, 10, 180 + idx).await;
   379	    }
   380	
   381	    let aggregates = aggregate_output_distribution(&fx.app_pool, tenant_id)
   382	        .await
   383	        .expect("aggregate output distribution");
   384	    assert_eq!(aggregates.len(), 1);
   385	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].sample_size_7d, Some(8));
   386	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].sample_size_30d, Some(16));
   387	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].baseline_sample_size, Some(8));
   388	
   389	    let mut tx = fx.app_pool.begin().await.expect("begin RLS read tx");
   390	    sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   391	        .bind(tenant_id.to_string())
   392	        .execute(&mut *tx)
   393	        .await
   394	        .expect("set RLS tenant");
   395	    let row = sqlx::query(
   396	        r#"
   397	        SELECT sample_size_7d, sample_size_30d
   398	        FROM output_distribution_cache
   399	        WHERE tenant_id = $1
   400	          AND model = 'gpt-4o-mini'
   401	          AND agent_id = 'agent-alpha'
   402	          AND prompt_class = 'chat_short'
   403	        "#,
   404	    )
   405	    .bind(tenant_id)
   406	    .fetch_one(&mut *tx)
   407	    .await
   408	    .expect("read cache row through RLS");
   409	    assert_eq!(row.get::<i32, _>("sample_size_7d"), 8);
   410	    assert_eq!(row.get::<i32, _>("sample_size_30d"), 16);
   411	    tx.commit().await.expect("commit RLS read tx");
   412	}
   413	
   414	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   415	async fn cycle_e2e_postgres_joins_sparse_outcomes_to_decision_mirrors() {
   416	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   417	        return;
   418	    };
   419	    let tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   420	
   421	    for idx in 0..4 {
   422	        seed_sparse_outcome_pair(&fx.owner_pool, tenant_id, idx, 1, 100 + idx).await;
   423	    }
   424	    for idx in 4..8 {
   425	        seed_sparse_outcome_pair(&fx.owner_pool, tenant_id, idx, 10, 180 + idx).await;
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    let aggregates = aggregate_output_distribution(&fx.app_pool, tenant_id)
   429	        .await
   430	        .expect("aggregate sparse outcome distribution");
   431	    assert_eq!(aggregates.len(), 1);
   432	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].model, "gpt-4o-mini");
   433	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].agent_id, "agent-alpha");
   434	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].prompt_class, "chat_short");
   435	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].sample_size_7d, Some(4));
   436	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].sample_size_30d, Some(8));
   437	    assert_eq!(aggregates[0].baseline_sample_size, Some(4));
   438	
   439	    let mut tx = fx.app_pool.begin().await.expect("begin RLS read tx");
   440	    sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   441	        .bind(tenant_id.to_string())
   442	        .execute(&mut *tx)
   443	        .await
   444	        .expect("set RLS tenant");
   445	    let rows: i64 = sqlx::query_scalar(
   446	        r#"
   447	        SELECT count(*)
   448	        FROM output_distribution_cache
   449	        WHERE tenant_id = $1
   450	          AND model = 'gpt-4o-mini'
   451	          AND agent_id = 'agent-alpha'
   452	          AND prompt_class = 'chat_short'
   453	        "#,
   454	    )
   455	    .bind(tenant_id)
   456	    .fetch_one(&mut *tx)
   457	    .await
   458	    .expect("read joined cache row through RLS");
   459	    assert_eq!(rows, 1);
   460	    tx.commit().await.expect("commit RLS read tx");
   461	}

   463	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   464	async fn rls_injection_blocks_cross_tenant_cache_reads_and_writes() {
   465	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   466	        return;
   467	    };
   468	    let tenant_a = Uuid::new_v4();
   469	    let tenant_b = Uuid::new_v4();
   470	
   471	    for idx in 0..4 {
   472	        seed_outcome_pair(&fx.owner_pool, tenant_a, idx, 1, 100 + idx).await;
   473	    }
   474	    aggregate_output_distribution(&fx.app_pool, tenant_a)
   475	        .await
   476	        .expect("aggregate tenant a");
   477	
   478	    let mut tx = fx.app_pool.begin().await.expect("begin tenant b tx");
   479	    sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
   480	        .bind(tenant_b.to_string())
   481	        .execute(&mut *tx)
   482	        .await
   483	        .expect("set RLS tenant b");
   484	
   485	    let visible: i64 =
   486	        sqlx::query_scalar("SELECT count(*) FROM output_distribution_cache WHERE tenant_id = $1")
   487	            .bind(tenant_a)
   488	            .fetch_one(&mut *tx)
   489	            .await
   490	            .expect("cross-tenant read count");
   491	    assert_eq!(visible, 0, "tenant B must not see tenant A cache rows");
   492	
   493	    let err = sqlx::query(
   494	        r#"
   495	        INSERT INTO output_distribution_cache (
   496	          tenant_id, model, agent_id, prompt_class,
   497	          sample_size_30d, computed_at, aggregation_version
   498	        )
   499	        VALUES ($1, 'gpt-4o-mini', 'agent-alpha', 'rag', 1, now(), 'v1alpha1')
   500	        "#,
   501	    )
   502	    .bind(tenant_a)
   503	    .execute(&mut *tx)
   504	    .await
   505	    .expect_err("RLS WITH CHECK must reject mismatched tenant write");
   506	    let msg = err.to_string();
   507	    assert!(
   508	        msg.contains("row-level security") || msg.contains("violates row-level security policy"),
   509	        "unexpected RLS error: {msg}"
   510	    );
   511	}

   513	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   514	async fn drift_alert_audit_row_can_land_without_prediction_mirror_columns() {
   515	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   516	        return;
   517	    };
   518	    let tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   519	    let event_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   520	
   521	    insert_global_key(
   522	        &fx.owner_pool,
   523	        event_id,
   524	        tenant_id,
   525	        None,
   526	        "spendguard.audit.prediction_drift_alert.v1alpha1",
   527	        0,
   528	    )
   529	    .await;
   530	    insert_canonical_event(CanonicalSeed {
   531	        pool: &fx.owner_pool,
   532	        event_id,
   533	        tenant_id,
   534	        decision_id: None,
   535	        run_id: None,
   536	        event_type: "spendguard.audit.prediction_drift_alert.v1alpha1",
   537	        seq: 9001,
   538	        age_days: 0,
   539	        actual_input_tokens: None,
   540	        actual_output_tokens: None,
   541	        model: None,
   542	        agent_id: None,
   543	        prompt_class: None,
   544	    })
   545	    .await;
   546	
   547	    let row = sqlx::query(
   548	        r#"
   549	        SELECT
   550	          producer_signature,
   551	          predicted_a_tokens, predicted_b_tokens, predicted_c_tokens,
   552	          actual_input_tokens, actual_output_tokens,
   553	          model, agent_id, prompt_class
   554	        FROM canonical_events
   555	        WHERE event_id = $1
   556	        "#,
   557	    )
   558	    .bind(event_id)
   559	    .fetch_one(&fx.owner_pool)
   560	    .await
   561	    .expect("read drift alert row");
   562	
   563	    assert!(!row.get::<Vec<u8>, _>("producer_signature").is_empty());
   564	    assert!(row
   565	        .try_get::<Option<i64>, _>("predicted_a_tokens")
   566	        .unwrap()
   567	        .is_none());
   568	    assert!(row
   569	        .try_get::<Option<i64>, _>("predicted_b_tokens")
   570	        .unwrap()
   571	        .is_none());
   572	    assert!(row
   573	        .try_get::<Option<i64>, _>("predicted_c_tokens")
   574	        .unwrap()
   575	        .is_none());
   576	    assert!(row
   577	        .try_get::<Option<i64>, _>("actual_input_tokens")
   578	        .unwrap()
   579	        .is_none());
   580	    assert!(row
   581	        .try_get::<Option<i64>, _>("actual_output_tokens")
   582	        .unwrap()
   583	        .is_none());
   584	    assert!(row.try_get::<Option<String>, _>("model").unwrap().is_none());
   585	    assert!(row
   586	        .try_get::<Option<String>, _>("agent_id")
   587	        .unwrap()
   588	        .is_none());
   589	    assert!(row
   590	        .try_get::<Option<String>, _>("prompt_class")
   591	        .unwrap()
   592	        .is_none());
   593	}

   595	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   596	async fn drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_is_key_and_tenant_scoped() {
   597	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   598	        return;
   599	    };
   600	    let store = PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore::new(fx.app_pool.clone());
   601	    let tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   602	    let now = Utc::now();
   603	    let key = DriftAlertKey {
   604	        tenant_id,
   605	        model: "gpt-4o-mini".into(),
   606	        agent_id: "agent-alpha".into(),
   607	        prompt_class: "chat_short".into(),
   608	    };
   609	
   610	    let first = store.check(&key, now).await.expect("first");
   611	    assert!(matches!(first, DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }));
   612	    store
   613	        .record_emitted(&key, now, 2.5)
   614	        .await
   615	        .expect("record first");
   616	
   617	    let duplicate = store
   618	        .check(&key, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   619	        .await
   620	        .expect("duplicate");
   621	    assert!(matches!(
   622	        duplicate,
   623	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Suppressed { .. }
   624	    ));
   625	
   626	    let mut different_prompt = key.clone();
   627	    different_prompt.prompt_class = "rag".into();
   628	    let prompt_decision = store
   629	        .check(&different_prompt, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   630	        .await
   631	        .expect("different prompt");
   632	    assert!(matches!(
   633	        prompt_decision,
   634	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   635	    ));
   636	
   637	    let mut different_model = key.clone();
   638	    different_model.model = "claude-3-5-sonnet".into();
   639	    let model_decision = store
   640	        .check(&different_model, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   641	        .await
   642	        .expect("different model");
   643	    assert!(matches!(
   644	        model_decision,
   645	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   646	    ));
   647	
   648	    let mut different_agent = key.clone();
   649	    different_agent.agent_id = "agent-beta".into();
   650	    let agent_decision = store
   651	        .check(&different_agent, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   652	        .await
   653	        .expect("different agent");
   654	    assert!(matches!(
   655	        agent_decision,
   656	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   657	    ));
   658	
   659	    let mut different_tenant = key.clone();
   660	    different_tenant.tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   661	    let tenant_decision = store
   662	        .check(&different_tenant, now + ChronoDuration::hours(1))
   663	        .await
   664	        .expect("different tenant");
   665	    assert!(matches!(
   666	        tenant_decision,
   667	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   668	    ));
   669	
   670	    let after_expiry = store
   671	        .check(&key, now + ChronoDuration::hours(25))
   672	        .await
   673	        .expect("after expiry");
   674	    assert!(matches!(
   675	        after_expiry,
   676	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   677	    ));
   678	}

   681	async fn drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_accepts_canonical_multibyte_agent_id() {
   682	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   683	        return;
   684	    };
   685	    let store = PostgresDriftAlertCooldownStore::new(fx.app_pool.clone());
   686	    let key = DriftAlertKey {
   687	        tenant_id: Uuid::new_v4(),
   688	        model: "gpt-4o-mini".into(),
   689	        agent_id: "客".repeat(128),
   690	        prompt_class: "chat_short".into(),
   691	    };
   692	
   693	    let decision = store
   694	        .check(&key, Utc::now())
   695	        .await
   696	        .expect("128-character multibyte agent_id is valid per canonical_events");
   697	    assert!(matches!(
   698	        decision,
   699	        DriftAlertCooldownDecision::Allowed { .. }
   700	    ));
   701	    store

   707	#[tokio::test(flavor = "multi_thread", worker_threads = 4)]
   708	async fn drift_alert_cooldown_postgres_rejects_non_finite_z_scores() {
   709	    let Some(fx) = setup_postgres().await else {
   710	        return;
   711	    };
   712	    let tenant_id = Uuid::new_v4();
   713	
   714	    for value in ["'NaN'::REAL", "'Infinity'::REAL", "'-Infinity'::REAL"] {
   715	        let mut tx = fx.app_pool.begin().await.expect("begin tx");

/bin/zsh -lc "sed -n '1,320p' services/stats_aggregator/src/aggregation.rs" in /Users/michael.chen/products/agentic-spendguard

//! Aggregation cycle SQL per stats-aggregator-spec-v1alpha1.md §4.1.
//!
//! ## Algorithm
//!
//! Per spec §4.1 the cycle:
//!   1. Acquire Postgres advisory lock (singleton — spec §2.2 + §8.3)
//!   2. For each tenant:
//!        - Run the main 7d+30d aggregation query, UPSERT into
//!          output_distribution_cache
//!        - Run the run-length aggregation query (spec §6), UPSERT into
//!          run_length_distribution_cache
//!        - Run drift detection per bucket (spec §7.1), emit
//!          prediction_drift_alert CloudEvents for buckets with
//!          |z_score| > drift_z_threshold AND sample_size_7d >=
//!          MIN_SAMPLES_FOR_ALERT
//!        - COMMIT per-tenant transaction
//!   3. Release advisory lock
//!
//! ## Per-tenant transaction
//!
//! Spec §8.3 — per-tenant commit ensures one tenant's failure doesn't
//! roll back other tenants' updates. The advisory lock guarantees no
//! other aggregator instance can interleave.
//!
//! ## RLS writer-side discipline (R2 B1)
//!
//! The aggregation writer needs to insert/update rows across all
//! tenants. RLS policy on output_distribution_cache + run_length_*
//! is FOR ALL (R2 B1) — every UPSERT is checked against
//! `app.current_tenant_id`. The writer therefore MUST invoke
//! `SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', '<tenant>', true)`
//! IMMEDIATELY after `pool.begin()` so the per-transaction GUC is
//! visible to subsequent SELECTs + UPSERTs. The R1 shape claimed
//! BYPASSRLS but the role attribute was never granted; FOR ALL +
//! SET LOCAL is the supported path going forward.

use anyhow::Context;
use sqlx::pool::PoolConnection;
use sqlx::postgres::{PgPool, Postgres};
use sqlx::Row;
use tracing::{debug, info};
use uuid::Uuid;

/// Identifier for the Postgres advisory lock per spec §8.3. Chosen as a
/// stable random i64 so concurrent stats_aggregator deployments
/// (e.g. blue-green rollout) compete for the same lock; only the lock
/// holder runs the cycle.
pub const STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID: i64 = 0x5350_4441_4747_5253_u64 as i64; // "SPDAGGRS"

/// One bucket's pre-computed aggregate as read back for drift detection.
///
/// R2 M2 (Software F5): drift_detector::compute_z_score must use a
/// baseline window that EXCLUDES the current 7d window. Spec §7.1:
///
/// ```text
/// baseline_mean = mean over [now - 30d, now - 7d]
/// baseline_stddev = stddev over [now - 30d, now - 7d]
/// current_mean = mean_7d
/// z = (current_mean - baseline_mean) / baseline_stddev
/// ```
///
/// Previously we naively used mean_30d (which INCLUDES the last 7 days)
/// as the baseline — the current window thus contributes to its own
/// reference, biasing z toward 0 and masking real drift. The R2 fix
/// adds dedicated baseline_* fields filled from a separate window query.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct BucketAggregate {
    pub tenant_id: Uuid,
    pub model: String,
    pub agent_id: String,
    pub prompt_class: String,
    pub mean_7d: Option<f32>,
    pub stddev_7d: Option<f32>,
    pub sample_size_7d: Option<i32>,
    pub mean_30d: Option<f32>,
    pub stddev_30d: Option<f32>,
    pub sample_size_30d: Option<i32>,
    /// R2 M2: window over [now - 30d, now - 7d] — baseline used by
    /// drift detector. Distinct from mean_30d (which is the full 30d
    /// window for Strategy B's cache lookup).
    pub baseline_mean: Option<f32>,
    pub baseline_stddev: Option<f32>,
    pub baseline_sample_size: Option<i32>,
}

/// Acquire the singleton advisory lock per spec §8.3 on a *pinned*
/// PoolConnection.
///
/// R2 B2 (Backend + Software + DB B3): `pg_try_advisory_lock` is
/// session-bound — releasing it on a different connection is a no-op.
/// The R1 shape called `pool.fetch_one()` (arbitrary checkout) for the
/// acquire and `pool.execute()` (different checkout) for the release,
/// so the lock leaked and every subsequent cycle skipped the cycle.
///
/// R2 returns the PoolConnection so the scheduler can hold it for the
/// entire cycle and explicitly release on the same connection. The
/// connection also serves any cycle-wide control queries (per-tenant
/// transactions are still checked out from the pool — `pool.begin()` —
/// because each tenant transaction needs its own commit boundary; the
/// advisory lock itself only needs to live on the pinned connection).
///
/// Returns:
///   * `Ok(Some(conn))` — lock acquired; caller proceeds with the cycle.
///     Caller MUST call [`release_lock_conn`] on the returned connection
///     when done.
///   * `Ok(None)` — another instance holds the lock; caller skips the
///     cycle and emits the stats_aggregator_skipped_lock_held metric.
///
/// Per spec §10 — Postgres session-level locks auto-release on session
/// disconnect, so a panicking scheduler doesn't permanently leak. TCP
/// keepalives govern stale-session detection (~ 2h Linux default;
/// operators tune via tcp_keepalives_idle on the Postgres side).
pub async fn try_acquire_lock_conn(
    pool: &PgPool,
) -> Result<Option<PoolConnection<Postgres>>, anyhow::Error> {
    let mut conn = pool
        .acquire()
        .await
        .context("acquire pool conn for advisory lock")?;
    let acquired: bool = sqlx::query_scalar("SELECT pg_try_advisory_lock($1)")
        .bind(STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID)
        .fetch_one(&mut *conn)
        .await
        .context("pg_try_advisory_lock")?;
    if acquired {
        info!(
            lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
            "acquired stats_aggregator advisory lock (pinned)"
        );
        Ok(Some(conn))
    } else {
        info!(
            lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
            "advisory lock held by another instance; skipping cycle"
        );
        // Drop the connection — return it to the pool. Postgres
        // pg_try_advisory_lock returns FALSE without taking the lock,
        // so there is nothing to release.
        drop(conn);
        Ok(None)
    }
}

/// Release the advisory lock on the connection that acquired it.
///
/// R2 B2: must run on the same session that called
/// `pg_try_advisory_lock` — Postgres bookkeeping is per-session. The
/// connection is then dropped (returned to the pool).
///
/// Failure to release is non-fatal: the lock will release when the
/// session disconnects (immediately on drop here, since we drop the
/// connection at the end). We still surface the error so operators see
/// any anomalies in the cycle metrics.
pub async fn release_lock_conn(mut conn: PoolConnection<Postgres>) -> Result<(), anyhow::Error> {
    sqlx::query("SELECT pg_advisory_unlock($1)")
        .bind(STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID)
        .execute(&mut *conn)
        .await
        .context("pg_advisory_unlock")?;
    debug!(
        lock_id = STATS_AGGREGATOR_ADVISORY_LOCK_ID,
        "released stats_aggregator advisory lock"
    );
    Ok(())
}

/// Discover the set of distinct tenants present in canonical_events for
/// the last 30 days. Per spec §8.3 we iterate per-tenant for transaction
/// isolation.
///
/// R2 B4: column is `ingest_at` (matches canonical_events.ingest_at —
/// insertion-time stamp) not `recorded_at`. R2 M7: add the
/// recorded_month partition-pruning predicate so the planner stays on
/// the active monthly partitions instead of scanning the default
/// partition.
pub async fn discover_active_tenants(pool: &PgPool) -> Result<Vec<Uuid>, anyhow::Error> {
    let rows = sqlx::query(
        r#"
        SELECT DISTINCT tenant_id
        FROM canonical_events
        WHERE event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
          AND ingest_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
          AND recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
        "#,
    )
    .fetch_all(pool)
    .await
    .context("discover_active_tenants")?;
    let tenants = rows
        .into_iter()
        .map(|r| r.get::<Uuid, _>("tenant_id"))
        .collect();
    Ok(tenants)
}

/// Run the main aggregation cycle for one tenant per spec §4.1. Inserts /
/// updates rows in output_distribution_cache. Returns the list of
/// post-update bucket aggregates so the drift detector can consume them.
pub async fn aggregate_output_distribution(
    pool: &PgPool,
    tenant_id: Uuid,
) -> Result<Vec<BucketAggregate>, anyhow::Error> {
    let mut tx = pool.begin().await.context("begin tenant tx")?;

    // R2 B1: set RLS session variable per migration 0016 FOR ALL policy.
    // Without this every UPSERT below would fail with "new row violates
    // row-level security policy". `set_config(..., true)` is the
    // SET-LOCAL flavour — the GUC is auto-reset at COMMIT / ROLLBACK.
    sqlx::query("SELECT set_config('app.current_tenant_id', $1, true)")
        .bind(tenant_id.to_string())
        .execute(&mut *tx)
        .await
        .context("set RLS tenant_id for output_distribution_cache")?;

    // Spec §4.1 main aggregation query. NOTE: we run two queries (7d
    // window + 30d window) and stitch via the application — keeping
    // the SQL simpler than the spec's CTE-with-LEFT-JOIN shape and
    // friendlier to per-tenant transaction commit semantics. The
    // production query plan benchmarks closer to the CTE form because
    // the percentile_cont workload is the dominant cost; the two-phase
    // application stitching adds ~5% overhead vs the full SQL CTE.
    //
    // R2 B3 (Software B4): GROUP BY the 7-class `prompt_class` enum —
    // NOT prompt_class_fingerprint. output-predictor spec §8.2 closing
    // paragraph: "Aggregator key uses class itself, not fingerprint —
    // fingerprint is the audit identifier, class is the aggregation
    // bucket." Stitching by the enum means the predictor's L4 cache
    // lookup (keyed on req.prompt_class) hits real rows.
    //
    // R2 B4 (DB B1): columns referenced are the first-class mirror
    // columns added in 0018 (model, agent_id, prompt_class) — NOT the
    // base64-decoded JSON path. ingest_at not recorded_at (matches the
    // real canonical_events.ingest_at). recorded_month partition-prune
    // predicate (R2 M7) pins the planner to active partitions.
    //
    // GA_07 R5 arbitration: sidecar commit/outcome rows are intentionally
    // sparse; the paired decision row is the authoritative source for
    // predictor bucket mirrors. Aggregate actual output tokens from
    // outcome rows, then join by decision_id to recover the decision's
    // (model, agent_id, prompt_class) when the outcome did not duplicate
    // those fields.
    let agg_30d = sqlx::query(
        r#"
        SELECT
          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
          percentile_cont(0.50) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p50_30d,
          percentile_cont(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p95_30d,
          percentile_cont(0.99) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p99_30d,
          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS mean_30d,
          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS stddev_30d,
          count(*)::INT AS sample_size_30d
        FROM canonical_events outcome
        LEFT JOIN canonical_events decision
          ON decision.tenant_id = outcome.tenant_id
         AND decision.decision_id = outcome.decision_id
         AND decision.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision'
         AND decision.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
        WHERE outcome.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
          AND outcome.actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL
          AND outcome.ingest_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
          AND outcome.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '30 days')::DATE
          AND outcome.tenant_id = $1
          AND COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) IS NOT NULL
          AND COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) IS NOT NULL
          AND COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) IS NOT NULL
        GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
        "#,
    )
    .bind(tenant_id)
    .fetch_all(&mut *tx)
    .await
    .context("aggregate 30d window")?;

    let agg_7d = sqlx::query(
        r#"
        SELECT
          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
          percentile_cont(0.50) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p50_7d,
          percentile_cont(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p95_7d,
          percentile_cont(0.99) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS p99_7d,
          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS mean_7d,
          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS stddev_7d,
          count(*)::INT AS sample_size_7d
        FROM canonical_events outcome
        LEFT JOIN canonical_events decision
          ON decision.tenant_id = outcome.tenant_id
         AND decision.decision_id = outcome.decision_id
         AND decision.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.decision'
         AND decision.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '7 days')::DATE
        WHERE outcome.event_type = 'spendguard.audit.outcome'
          AND outcome.actual_output_tokens IS NOT NULL
          AND outcome.ingest_at >= now() - interval '7 days'
          AND outcome.recorded_month >= DATE_TRUNC('month', now() - interval '7 days')::DATE
          AND outcome.tenant_id = $1
          AND COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) IS NOT NULL
          AND COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) IS NOT NULL
          AND COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) IS NOT NULL
        GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
        "#,
    )
    .bind(tenant_id)
    .fetch_all(&mut *tx)
    .await
    .context("aggregate 7d window")?;

    // R2 M2: drift baseline — distinct window [now-30d, now-7d] that
    // EXCLUDES the current 7d so the baseline doesn't contaminate the
    // z-score. Same column shape as the other two queries.
    let agg_baseline = sqlx::query(
        r#"
        SELECT
          COALESCE(outcome.model, decision.model) AS model,
          COALESCE(outcome.agent_id, decision.agent_id) AS agent_id,
          COALESCE(outcome.prompt_class, decision.prompt_class) AS prompt_class,
          avg(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS baseline_mean,
          stddev_samp(outcome.actual_output_tokens)::REAL AS baseline_stddev,

exec
/bin/zsh -lc "sed -n '260,620p' services/canonical_ingest/src/handlers/append_events.rs" in /Users/michael.chen/products/agentic-spendguard
 succeeded in 0ms:
    // silently fall back to Utc::now() (mutates the canonical event).
    let event_time = match &evt.time {
        Some(Timestamp { seconds, nanos }) => {
            if *nanos < 0 || *nanos >= 1_000_000_000 {
                return error_result(
                    &evt.id,
                    EventStatus::Quarantined,
                    DomainError::InvalidRequest(format!(
                        "event_time.nanos {} out of [0, 1_000_000_000)",
                        nanos
                    )),
                );
            }
            match chrono::DateTime::<Utc>::from_timestamp(*seconds, *nanos as u32) {
                Some(t) => t,
                None => {
                    return error_result(
                        &evt.id,
                        EventStatus::Quarantined,
                        DomainError::InvalidRequest(format!(
                            "event_time seconds {} out of range",
                            seconds
                        )),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        None => {
            return error_result(
                &evt.id,
                EventStatus::Quarantined,
                DomainError::InvalidRequest("event_time required".into()),
            );
        }
    };

    // Build append input.
    let payload_json =
        serde_json::to_value(cloudevent_to_json(evt)).unwrap_or(serde_json::Value::Null);
    let event_hash = Sha256::digest(canonical_bytes(evt)).to_vec();

    // Cost Advisor P1.5 (issue #51, spec §5.1.2): classify audit
    // .outcome events into one of the 9 failure_class enum values.
    // For non-outcome events the classifier returns None and we
    // persist NULL in canonical_events.failure_class. The classifier
    // is fault-tolerant: malformed data_b64 maps to FailureClass
    // ::Unknown rather than aborting the INSERT.
    let decoded_data = crate::classify::decode_payload_data(&payload_json);
    let failure_class = crate::classify::classify_audit_outcome(&evt.r#type, decoded_data.as_ref())
        .map(|c| c.as_db_str());
    let aggregator = aggregator_mirrors_from_event(evt, decoded_data.as_ref(), run_id);

    let input = AppendInput {
        event_id,
        tenant_id,
        decision_id,
        run_id,
        event_type: &evt.r#type,
        storage_class,
        producer_id: &evt.producer_id,
        producer_sequence,
        producer_signature: &evt.producer_signature,
        signing_key_id: &evt.signing_key_id,
        event_hash: &event_hash,
        schema_bundle_id: bundle.schema_bundle_id,
        schema_bundle_hash: &bundle.schema_bundle_hash,
        specversion: &evt.specversion,
        source: &evt.source,
        event_time,
        datacontenttype: &evt.datacontenttype,
        payload_json,
        payload_blob_ref: None,
        region_id: &cfg.region,
        ingest_shard_id: &cfg.ingest_shard_id,
        failure_class,
        model: aggregator.model,
        agent_id: aggregator.agent_id,
        run_id_mirror: aggregator.run_id_mirror,
        prompt_class: aggregator.prompt_class,
        prompt_class_fingerprint: aggregator.prompt_class_fingerprint,
        prediction: prediction_columns_from_event(evt),
    };

    // Per-decision sequence enforcement: audit.outcome with no preceding decision.
    if evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.outcome" {
        let dec_id = match decision_id {
            Some(d) => d,
            None => {
                return error_result(
                    &evt.id,
                    EventStatus::Quarantined,
                    DomainError::InvalidRequest("audit.outcome missing decision_id".into()),
                );
            }
        };

        match append::has_preceding_decision(pool, tenant_id, dec_id).await {
            Ok(true) => { /* fall through to normal append */ }
            Ok(false) => {
                let orphan_after =
                    Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(cfg.orphan_after_seconds as i64);
                if let Err(e) =
                    append::quarantine_audit_outcome(pool, input.clone(), orphan_after).await
                {
                    return error_result(&evt.id, EventStatus::Quarantined, e);
                }
                return EventResult {
                    event_id: evt.id.clone(),
                    status: EventStatus::AwaitingPrecedingDecision as i32,
                    ingest_position: None,
                    error: None,
                };
            }
            Err(e) => return error_result(&evt.id, EventStatus::Quarantined, e),
        }
    }

    // Normal append.
    match append::append_event(pool, input).await {
        Ok(AppendOutcome::Appended { ingest_log_offset }) => {
            debug!(
                event_id = %evt.id,
                offset = ingest_log_offset,
                storage_class = ?storage_class,
                "appended"
            );

            // After committing an audit.decision row, release any
            // quarantined audit.outcome rows for the same decision_id.
            // Release function uses original quarantine metadata (NOT this
            // decision's bundle / datacontenttype).
            if evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.decision" {
                if let Some(dec) = decision_id {
                    if let Err(e) = append::release_quarantined_outcomes(
                        pool,
                        tenant_id,
                        dec,
                        &cfg.region,
                        &cfg.ingest_shard_id,
                    )
                    .await
                    {
                        warn!(
                            decision_id = %dec,
                            err = %e,
                            "release_quarantined_outcomes failed; reaper will retry"
                        );
                    }
                }
            }

            EventResult {
                event_id: evt.id.clone(),
                status: EventStatus::Appended as i32,
                ingest_position: Some(IngestPosition {
                    region_id: cfg.region.clone(),
                    ingest_shard_id: cfg.ingest_shard_id.clone(),
                    ingest_log_offset: ingest_log_offset as u64,
                }),
                error: None,
            }
        }
        Ok(AppendOutcome::Deduped) => {
            metrics.inc_deduped(route_to_metric(route));
            EventResult {
                event_id: evt.id.clone(),
                status: EventStatus::Deduped as i32,
                ingest_position: None,
                error: None,
            }
        }
        Err(DomainError::Duplicate(msg)) => EventResult {
            event_id: evt.id.clone(),
            status: EventStatus::Duplicate as i32,
            ingest_position: None,
            error: Some(ProtoError {
                code: ProtoCode::DuplicateDecisionEvent as i32,
                message: msg,
                details: Default::default(),
            }),
        },
        Err(DomainError::AwaitingPrecedingDecision(msg)) => {
            // Defense-in-depth: trigger fired despite our check above; redirect
            // to quarantine. This can happen if a concurrent caller deleted
            // the decision (which our triggers forbid, but kept here for
            // safety).
            warn!(event_id = %evt.id, reason = %msg, "trigger-side quarantine fallback");
            let orphan_after =
                Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(cfg.orphan_after_seconds as i64);
            // Rebuild input — original was moved.
            let payload_json =
                serde_json::to_value(cloudevent_to_json(evt)).unwrap_or(serde_json::Value::Null);
            // Re-classify for the quarantine path's audit row.
            let decoded_data = crate::classify::decode_payload_data(&payload_json);
            let failure_class =
                crate::classify::classify_audit_outcome(&evt.r#type, decoded_data.as_ref())
                    .map(|c| c.as_db_str());
            let aggregator = aggregator_mirrors_from_event(evt, decoded_data.as_ref(), run_id);
            let input = AppendInput {
                event_id,
                tenant_id,
                decision_id,
                run_id,
                event_type: &evt.r#type,
                storage_class,
                producer_id: &evt.producer_id,
                producer_sequence,
                producer_signature: &evt.producer_signature,
                signing_key_id: &evt.signing_key_id,
                event_hash: &event_hash,
                schema_bundle_id: bundle.schema_bundle_id,
                schema_bundle_hash: &bundle.schema_bundle_hash,
                specversion: &evt.specversion,
                source: &evt.source,
                event_time,
                datacontenttype: &evt.datacontenttype,
                payload_json,
                payload_blob_ref: None,
                region_id: &cfg.region,
                ingest_shard_id: &cfg.ingest_shard_id,
                failure_class,
                model: aggregator.model,
                agent_id: aggregator.agent_id,
                run_id_mirror: aggregator.run_id_mirror,
                prompt_class: aggregator.prompt_class,
                prompt_class_fingerprint: aggregator.prompt_class_fingerprint,
                prediction: prediction_columns_from_event(evt),
            };
            if let Err(e) = append::quarantine_audit_outcome(pool, input, orphan_after).await {
                return error_result(&evt.id, EventStatus::Quarantined, e);
            }
            EventResult {
                event_id: evt.id.clone(),
                status: EventStatus::AwaitingPrecedingDecision as i32,
                ingest_position: None,
                error: None,
            }
        }
        Err(e) => error_result(&evt.id, EventStatus::Quarantined, e),
    }
}

fn validate_envelope(evt: &CloudEvent) -> Result<(), DomainError> {
    if evt.specversion != "1.0" {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest(format!(
            "specversion must be '1.0', got '{}'",
            evt.specversion
        )));
    }
    if evt.r#type.is_empty() {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest("type required".into()));
    }
    if evt.id.is_empty() {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest("id required".into()));
    }
    if evt.tenant_id.is_empty() {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest("tenant_id required".into()));
    }
    if evt.producer_id.is_empty() {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest("producer_id required".into()));
    }
    // decision_id is REQUIRED for audit chain events. Without it, the
    // partial UNIQUE indexes on (tenant_id, decision_id) cannot enforce
    // per-decision uniqueness because Postgres treats multiple NULLs as
    // distinct.
    if (evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.decision" || evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.outcome")
        && evt.decision_id.is_empty()
    {
        return Err(DomainError::InvalidRequest(format!(
            "{} requires non-empty decision_id",
            evt.r#type
        )));
    }
    Ok(())
}

fn cloudevent_to_json(evt: &CloudEvent) -> serde_json::Value {
    use base64::Engine as _;
    serde_json::json!({
        "specversion":     evt.specversion,
        "type":            evt.r#type,
        "source":          evt.source,
        "id":              evt.id,
        "time_seconds":    evt.time.as_ref().map(|t| t.seconds).unwrap_or_default(),
        "time_nanos":      evt.time.as_ref().map(|t| t.nanos).unwrap_or_default(),
        "datacontenttype": evt.datacontenttype,
        "data_b64":        base64::engine::general_purpose::STANDARD.encode(&evt.data),
        "tenantid":        evt.tenant_id,
        "runid":           evt.run_id,
        "decisionid":      evt.decision_id,
        "schema_bundle_id": evt.schema_bundle_id,
        "producer_id":     evt.producer_id,
        "producer_sequence": evt.producer_sequence,
        "signing_key_id":  evt.signing_key_id,
        "predicted_a_tokens": evt.predicted_a_tokens,
        "predicted_b_tokens": evt.predicted_b_tokens,
        "predicted_c_tokens": evt.predicted_c_tokens,
        "reserved_strategy": evt.reserved_strategy,
        "prediction_strategy_used": evt.prediction_strategy_used,
        "prediction_policy_used": evt.prediction_policy_used,
        "tokenizer_tier": evt.tokenizer_tier,
        "tokenizer_version_id": evt.tokenizer_version_id,
        "prediction_confidence": evt.prediction_confidence,
        "prediction_sample_size": evt.prediction_sample_size,
        "cold_start_layer_used": evt.cold_start_layer_used,
        "run_projection_at_decision_atomic": evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic,
        "run_predicted_remaining_steps": evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps,
        "run_steps_completed_so_far": evt.run_steps_completed_so_far,
        "actual_input_tokens": evt.actual_input_tokens,
        "actual_output_tokens": evt.actual_output_tokens,
        "delta_b_ratio": evt.delta_b_ratio,
        "delta_c_ratio": evt.delta_c_ratio,
    })
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, Default)]
struct AggregatorMirrors<'a> {
    model: Option<&'a str>,
    agent_id: Option<&'a str>,
    run_id_mirror: Option<Uuid>,
    prompt_class: Option<&'a str>,
    prompt_class_fingerprint: Option<&'a str>,
}

fn aggregator_mirrors_from_event<'a>(
    evt: &CloudEvent,
    decoded_data: Option<&'a serde_json::Value>,
    run_id: Option<Uuid>,
) -> AggregatorMirrors<'a> {
    if evt.r#type != "spendguard.audit.decision" && evt.r#type != "spendguard.audit.outcome" {
        return AggregatorMirrors::default();
    }
    let Some(data) = decoded_data.and_then(|v| v.as_object()) else {
        return AggregatorMirrors::default();
    };
    let model = json_nonempty_str(data.get("model"))
        .or_else(|| json_nonempty_str(data.get("model_family")));
    AggregatorMirrors {
        model,
        agent_id: json_nonempty_str(data.get("agent_id")),
        run_id_mirror: run_id,
        prompt_class: json_nonempty_str(data.get("prompt_class")),
        prompt_class_fingerprint: json_nonempty_str(data.get("prompt_class_fingerprint")),
    }
}

fn json_nonempty_str(value: Option<&serde_json::Value>) -> Option<&str> {
    value
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .map(str::trim)
        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
}

fn prediction_columns_from_event(evt: &CloudEvent) -> append::PredictionColumns<'_> {
    let is_decision = evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.decision";
    let is_outcome = evt.r#type == "spendguard.audit.outcome";
    let projector_unreachable = evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic == 0
        && evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps == -1
        && evt.run_steps_completed_so_far == 0;
    let projector_absent_default = evt.run_projection_at_decision_atomic == 0
        && evt.run_predicted_remaining_steps == 0
